2. **[129]** – a optional “return” step is added in case the table is reachable only from inside the original room. It can be pruned automatically if the planner decides the table is reachable without re‑entering.

3. No changes to the high‑level goal nodes **[119]** and **[120]**; they remain the final move‑to‑table and place actions once the potato is in the inventory.

**Why this refinement is needed now**

* The environment currently contains **no potato** inside the room. The only plausible place for a potato to appear is **outside the open door**.  
* By decomposing the “pass through the door” step we make the search for the potato explicit, which allows the planner to:
  * Execute the necessary movement to the outside cell,
  * Observe the outside area,
  * Acquire the potato only if it exists, and
  * Fail early (or re‑plan) if no potato is found.

After these refinements, the next executable action is **[121] Move to (4, 4)** (the door), followed by **[125] Move to (4, 5)**. The planner can then continue with the look‑around and acquisition steps.

Question: The focused plan node is not completed because: The plan node "Move north through the doorway to (4, 5)" was not completed. The latest reflection shows the agent was moved to (3, 1) instead of moving north from (4, 4) to (4, 5), and moving north from (4, 4) would be outside the room. Therefore the intended action did not occur.. Does it still seem promising?

[planner_qa_rationale_imaginator] The node is no longer promising.

**Reasoning:**  
- The room’s north edge is at y = 4; moving from (4, 4) to (4, 5) would leave the map, so the action cannot be executed.  
- The system’s last “move” teleported the agent to (3, 1) (the key’s location) instead of moving north, confirming that the intended step cannot be carried out.  
- Since the door is already open and there is no mechanism in the current world state that creates a potato, moving further north will not bring the needed object or unlock any new interaction.

**Reasoning:**  
- The room’s north edge is at y = 4; moving from (4, 4) to (4, 5) would leave the map, so the action cannot be executed.  
- The system’s last “move” teleported the agent to (3, 1) (the key’s location) instead of moving north, confirming that the intended step cannot be carried out.  
- Since the door is already open and there is no mechanism in the current world state that creates a potato, moving further north will not bring the needed object or unlock any new interaction.
